msg:advantage:
1. The facilities are new and the service is good. It opened at the end of September 2022. It has just opened for a month. The service staff at the front desk and restaurant are very good, young and enthusiastic. They are the kind of serious and well-organized service that has just joined the work. It is very good!
2. The environment is good. In the small road opposite the Moganshan Art Museum, there is a gas station at the intersection. The hotel park is like a big garden, quiet and large, with its own greenhouse and research base. Suitable for individual self-driving tour or study tour group.

shortcoming:
1. The breakfast is not good. Checking in on weekdays in off-season, it is understandable that there is no buffet breakfast, but there are few types of set meals, fixed food, and you cannot choose. There are only shredded pork noodles with pickled vegetables. After communication, the porridge will be provided the next day. The tea is only black tea. Since it is teabag, why canâ€™t there be green tea and scented tea? In short, there is no choice. But the quality of the food is good, the juice is from Huiyuan, it is chilled to keep fresh, and there is milk.
2. The No. 2 building where I live has several problems with the design of the bathroom: there is no place to hang bathrobes. There is no soap tray on the sink. The most serious problem is that the chandelier will knock on the head.
3. The gym locks the door at night. I didn't bother to find the front desk to open it. During the epidemic period, there were few people and it was understandable that the facilities could not be used.

All in all, the hardware is very good, and the service is also good, but some details still need to be improved, take your time, after all, it is still in the running-in period when it just opened.
